Defines bit arrays for valid characters in different header components\\n   - Used to prevent header injection by rejecting invalid characters\\n   - Supports per-protocol validation (HTTP/1.1 vs HTTP/2)\\n\\n## Path Normalization\\n\\n1. **Path Normalizer** (`source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/path_normalizer.h/cc`):\\n   - `checkForPercent00InUrlPath()` - prevents null byte injection via percent-encoding\\n\\n## Configuration and Overrides\\n\\n1. **Header Validator Configuration** (`source/extensions/http/header_validators/envoy_default/config.h/cc`):\\n   -
